---

## Pass 2: Special Character Names
A second pass was needed because names containing special characters (!, ?, &) were not caught by the initial regex pattern. This pass fixed 16 additional files with 55 corrections, primarily underscore-to-space conversions in names like `quote.HEIR_OF_GOD!` -> `quote.HEIR OF GOD!` and `thought.INVITE_OR_COMMAND?` -> `thought.INVITE OR COMMAND?`.

### Pass 2 Summary
- **Additional files modified**: 16
- **Additional corrections**: 55
- **Categories**: Underscore in name field (Rule 4c), Underscore in edge name (Rule 4c), Alias ALL CAPS (Rule 5b), en_title casing/prefix (Rule 9b)

### Post-Audit Validation
All categories show **zero remaining violations**:
- 0 underscore violations in name fields
- 0 duplicate alias prefixes
- 0 `b.edge.` misuse on PASSAGE files
- 0 underscores in edge names
- 0 escaped quotes in values
